The main capture methods are:\r\n\r\n‚Ä¢ Fullscreen\r\n‚Ä¢ Active window\r\n‚Ä¢ Active monitor\r\n‚Ä¢ Window menu\r\n‚Ä¢ Monitor menu\r\n‚Ä¢ Region\r\n‚Ä¢ Region (Light)\r\n‚Ä¢ Region (Transparent)\r\n‚Ä¢ Last region\r\n‚Ä¢ Custom region\r\n‚Ä¢ Screen recording\r\n‚Ä¢ Screen recording (GIF)\r\n‚Ä¢ Scrolling capture\r\n‚Ä¢ Webpage capture\r\n‚Ä¢ Text capture (OCR)\r\n‚Ä¢ Auto capture\r\n\r\nThere are many configurable screen capture settings such as showing the cursor, transparent window capture, delayed capture, multiple region selection with different shapes, etc.\r\n\r\nAfter the capture the following automated tasks can be executed:\r\n\r\n‚Ä¢ Show quick task menu\r\n‚Ä¢ Show \"After capture\" window\r\n‚Ä¢ Add image effects / watermark\r\n‚Ä¢ Annotate image\r\n‚Ä¢ Copy image to clipboard\r\n‚Ä¢ Print image\r\n‚Ä¢ Save image to file\r\n‚Ä¢ Save image to file as...\r\n‚Ä¢ Save thumbnail image to file\r\n‚Ä¢ Perform actions\r\n‚Ä¢ Copy file to clipboard\r\n‚Ä¢ Copy file path to clipboard\r\n‚Ä¢ Show file in explorer\r\n‚Ä¢ Recognize text (OCR)\r\n‚Ä¢ Show \"Before upload\" window\r\n‚Ä¢ Upload image to host\r\n‚Ä¢ Delete file locally\r\n\r\nFor example, the captured image can be opened in image annotator and after that, the image can be automatically saved to the hard disk and uploaded to your destination of choice.\r\n\r\nShareX allows you to upload any type of files with these methods:\r\n\r\n‚Ä¢ Upload file\r\n‚Ä¢ Upload folder\r\n‚Ä¢ Upload from clipboard\r\n‚Ä¢ Upload from URL\r\n‚Ä¢ Drag and drop upload\r\n‚Ä¢ Upload from Windows shell context menu\r\n‚Ä¢ Upload from Windows send to menu\r\n‚Ä¢ Watch folder\r\n\r\nAfter the upload, any of the following automated tasks can be executed:\r\n\r\n‚Ä¢ Show \"After upload\" window\r\n‚Ä¢ Shorten URL\r\n‚Ä¢ Share URL\r\n‚Ä¢ Copy URL to clipboard\r\n‚Ä¢ Open URL\r\n‚Ä¢ Show QR code window\r\n\r\nFor example, the uploaded image URL
